### [136] [The One-Word Census: Answer-Choice Conformity Across 44 Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12796)
*Tapan Parikh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 44个语言模型在被要求从大量有效选项中选择一个单词时，表现出显著的趋同现象。例如，在‘随便选一个词’的指令下，41%的模型选择了‘serendipity’。研究通过31个单轮提示（如‘说出一种树’），每模型执行四次，不使用系统提示，以精确匹配归一化标记的方式分析结果。使用‘答案选择意外度’（surprisal）评分模型：基于其他所有模型的联合答案分布，计算某模型答案的$-\log_2$概率。结果显示，7个类别中有一个答案占比超过80%，且模型间的趋同程度差异超过四倍，结构清晰——个人化和社区调优模型最不一致，最新主流旗舰模型最趋同，几乎不产生其他模型未给出的答案。在Claude、GPT、Qwen、Grok四个系列中，趋同性随代际上升，但最新旗舰版的Claude和GPT出现反向趋势，或暗示顶级模型战略调整。模型排名对组合变化鲁棒（留一家庭外相关系数0.985）。与人类类别生成习惯相比，模型在20个共享类别中有18个更集中。所有提示、转录和代码均公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究当语言模型面对大量等效答案时，是否倾向于选择相同答案，以及这种趋同现象的强度和结构特征。旨在揭示模型间行为一致性背后的机制，尤其是不同模型类型和版本之间的差异。

Method: 设计并实施‘一词普查’（One-Word Census）实验：使用31个单轮提示，每个提示对应一个具有多个合理答案的类别（如‘说出一种树’），每模型执行四次测试，无系统提示。答案以精确匹配归一化令牌的方式分析，不依赖嵌入或人工判断。使用留一法计算各模型答案的意外度（surprisal），即其答案在其他模型联合分布下的负对数概率。

Result: 模型表现出极端趋同：7个类别中一个答案占据超80%的响应；模型间趋同程度差异超过四倍，且结构分明：个人化/社区调优模型最不一致，最新主流旗舰模型最趋同，几乎不输出独特答案。在四大系列（Claude、GPT、Qwen、Grok）中，趋同性随代际提升，但最新旗舰版（Claude、GPT）出现趋同下降，可能预示战略转向。模型排名高度稳定（留一家庭外相关系数0.985）。与人类行为相比，模型在18/20共享类别中表现更集中。所有数据与代码公开。

Conclusion: 语言模型在自由选择任务中展现出高度且结构化的趋同行为。‘一词普查’工具揭示了模型间一致性模式，并暴露了模型类型、训练策略与代际演化的影响。最新旗舰模型出现趋同减弱趋势，或反映其在竞争格局中的再定位。该研究为理解大模型内在偏好与群体行为提供了可复现、低成本、高透明的分析框架。

Abstract: When a language model must pick one answer from a large space of equally valid options, which does it pick -- and how often is it the same answer every other model picks? Asked to "pick a word -- any word," 44 models chose "serendipity" 41% of the time. We characterize this convergence with a deliberately minimal instrument: 31 single-turn prompts, each naming a category with many valid one-word answers ("Name a tree."), asked four times per model with no system prompt. Analysis is exact-match on normalized tokens -- no embeddings, no judge -- at about a dollar per model. That models converge is well documented; our contribution is the instrument itself -- the One-Word Census -- and what it reveals about the structure of the convergence. We score each model by answer-choice surprisal: the average $-\log2$ probability of its answers under the pooled answers of all other models, leave-one-out. Convergence is extreme -- in 7 of 31 categories one answer takes over 80% of all answers -- yet conformity varies more than fourfold across models, and the variation is structured. Persona- and community-tuned models are the most divergent; the newest mainline flagships are the most conformist, producing almost no answer no other model gave. Within four lineages (Claude, GPT, Qwen, Grok) conformity rises with each generation -- but reverses for the latest flagship Claude and GPT models, a possible early signal of repositioning at the top tier. Rankings are robust to roster composition (leave-one-family-out rho = 0.985). Against human category-production norms, the field is more concentrated than people in 18 of 20 shared categories. All prompts, transcripts, and code are public.

</details>


### [137] [Knowledgeless Language Models: Suppressing Parametric Recall for Evidence-Grounded Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12831)
*Roi Cohen,Yvan Carré,Nick Lechtenbörger,Hendrik Droste,Lucas Kerschke,Russa Biswas,Gerard de Melo,Jan Buys*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为知识-较少语言模型（KLLMs）的新训练范式，通过在预训练数据中匿名化命名实体，消除基于实体的事实监督信号，从而减少模型对参数化记忆的依赖，增强其对上下文证据的依赖。实验表明，KLLMs在需要上下文推理的任务上表现更优，尤其在检索不完善的场景下展现出更强的鲁棒性和性能提升（最高相对增益20–25%），同时具有更好的校准性与可靠的拒绝回答行为。该研究证明：预训练阶段控制知识获取可有效引导模型向更可信、更依赖外部证据的方向演进，为构建可靠的语言模型提供新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型虽蕴含大量事实知识，但其参数化记忆易导致过时、不完整或与上下文冲突的问题，影响可靠性。因此亟需一种方法使模型更依赖外部证据而非内部记忆，以提升在真实场景下的表现。

Method: 提出知识-较少语言模型（KLLMs），在预训练阶段使用经过命名实体匿名化的语料库进行训练，从而削弱实体关联的事实监督，迫使模型减少对参数化知识的依赖，转向基于上下文证据的推理。

Result: KLLMs在闭卷事实召回上显著下降，但在需上下文信息的任务（如上下文问答、事实验证、幻觉检测）上表现优于基线模型；在检索不完善的情况下，相对提升达20–25%；具备更好的校准性（ECE、Brier得分、AUROC改善）和更可靠的拒绝回答行为。

Conclusion: 通过预训练阶段抑制实体关联的监督信号，可系统性引导模型从依赖参数化知识转向依赖外部证据，实现更可靠、更具鲁棒性的推理行为，为构建高可信度语言模型提供了新的基础范式。

Abstract: Language models encode substantial factual knowledge in their parameters, which can lead to unreliable behavior when this knowledge is outdated, incomplete, or misaligned with the provided context. In this work, we study whether modifying the pretraining signal can systematically shift models away from parametric recall and toward evidence-grounded reasoning. We introduce Knowledge--''Less'' Language Models (KLLMs), a fundamentally different epistemic training paradigm for LLMs, which are pretrained on corpora in which named entities are anonymized, thereby removing a primary channel for entity-linked factual supervision. This intervention substantially reduces closed-book factual recall, while often improving performance on tasks where relevant information is provided as context. Across multiple model scales, KLLMs consistently outperform matched baselines on contextual question answering, fact verification, and hallucination detection benchmarks. Crucially, in retrieval-grounded settings with imperfect evidence, KLLMs show improved robustness and achieve up to 20--25\% relative gains over standard language models. They further exhibit better calibration, with improved ECE, Brier score, and AUROC, as well as more reliable abstention behavior. Our results demonstrate that suppressing entity-linked supervision during pretraining induces a shift in epistemic behavior: KLLMs rely less on parametric knowledge and more on external evidence, leading to improved reliability under realistic conditions. This suggests that pretraining-time control over knowledge acquisition can complement retrieval-augmented and tool-based systems by providing a more evidence-sensitive base model.

Abstract: Rubric-based evaluation is a promising approach for assessing open-ended outputs from LLM-based research agents, particularly in paper reproduction, where direct paper-to-repository comparison is prone to hallucination. However, constructing paper-specific rubrics requires substantial expert effort, limiting the scalability of benchmarks such as PaperBench. In this work, we present, to our knowledge, the first systematic meta-evaluation of LLM-generated rubrics for paper reproduction. We reformulate rubrics into a checklist-style format and evaluate four generation settings across two backbone models. We meta-evaluate generated rubrics intrinsically by semantic similarity and extrinsically by score alignment with ground-truth rubrics. Our results show that the augmented settings substantially improves downstream evaluation alignment, with the strongest setting approaching the human baseline, while intrinsic gains are more modest. Further analyses reveal that LLM-generated rubrics are often overly fine-grained, biased toward high scores, and less adaptive to paper domains, highlighting both the affordances and limitations.

### [139] [Evaluating Large Language Models on Misconceptions in Multi-Turn Medical Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12884)
*Monica Munnangi,Saiph Savage*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出ThReadMed-QA数据集，用于评估大语言模型在多轮医疗对话中识别并纠正患者错误认知的能力。实验发现，即使前沿模型在单轮中表现良好，其纠错能力在后续对话轮次中显著下降，主要受错误传播影响，且即便上下文正确，性能仍不理想，凸显了现有评估框架的不足，并强调需建立更完善的多轮交互评估体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前评估框架无法捕捉大语言模型在包含错误假设或误解的多轮医疗对话中的行为，而这类对话在真实医患交流中常见，因此亟需一个能系统评估模型在多轮语境下纠正误解能力的新框架与数据集。

Method: 构建ThReadMed-QA多轮医疗对话数据集（2,437个对话线程，8,204个问答对），基于真实患者提问；采用基于评分标准的LLM-as-a-Judge框架，评估五个大语言模型在多轮互动中识别和纠正错误信念的表现，并通过模拟“最优上下文”（oracle分析）分离错误传播的影响。

Result: 尽管GPT-5和Claude-Haiku在初始问题中可纠正约85%的错误前提，但在两个后续追问后准确率降至约50%；即使使用医生原始回复替换模型输出以消除错误传播，性能仍不理想，表明模型在长期对话中存在持续性退化，存在潜在安全风险。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型在多轮医疗对话中难以稳定纠正患者误解，尤其在后续轮次中表现显著下降，说明现有评估方法不足以反映真实临床交互场景，亟需开发能捕捉多轮动态行为的新型评估体系，以保障患者导向型应用的安全性与可靠性。

Abstract: Patients seeking medical information often ask questions that embed incorrect assumptions or misconceptions. In such cases, safe medical communication requires not only answering the question, but identifying and correcting the underlying false belief. These interactions naturally unfold over multiple turns, a pattern now mirrored in interactions with LLMs. Yet current evaluation frameworks do not capture model behavior in these settings, where misconceptions can emerge, persist, or evolve over the course of a conversation. Whether LLMs can reliably correct such misconceptions over time remains largely unexamined. To study this, we introduce ThReadMed-QA, a multi-turn medical dialogue dataset of 2,437 patient-physician conversation threads comprising 8,204 question-answer pairs, derived from real patient interactions on AskDocs. This dataset enables systematic evaluation of whether models can detect and correct misconceptions under a multi-turn context. We evaluate five LLMs using a rubric-based LLM-as-a-Judge framework that scores responses based on their ability to identify and correct misconceptions. Our experiments reveal a consistent pattern: even frontier models that can address misconceptions in a single interaction degrade substantially over subsequent turns. GPT-5 and Claude-Haiku correct these false presuppositions around 85% on initial questions but drop to roughly 50% within two follow-ups. An oracle analysis replacing prior model outputs with physician responses shows that much of the degradation is driven by error propagation, while performance remains imperfect even under correct context. Even when models tend to correct misconceptions initially, their performance degrades substantially over later turns, leading to inconsistent and potentially unsafe guidance in patient-facing settings and highlighting the need for evaluation frameworks that capture multi-turn behavior.

</details>


### [140] [LLM Judges Can Be Too Generous When There Is No Reference Answer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12885)
*Chalamalasetti Kranti,Sowmya Vajjala*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLM）在无参考设置下评估开放式模型响应的可靠性。通过两个阶段的实验：一是校准实验，评估判别模型对任务的理解程度；二是敏感性实验，分析参考答案在提示中的存在与位置对判别模型性能的影响。结果显示，当缺乏参考答案时，判别模型倾向于高估错误答案，而引入参考答案后，其判断正确率可变化高达85%。与部分人类标注结果对比表明，这种由参考答案驱动的变化与人类判断一致。研究强调在无参考场景中使用前需对LLM判别器进行基于参考感知评估的校准，并提供了可复用的方法论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前越来越多地使用大型语言模型作为判别器来评估开放式生成模型的输出，尤其在缺乏真实答案参考的无参考评估场景中。然而，这些判别器是否真正具备可靠评估能力仍不明确，尤其在缺少参考答案的情况下是否存在偏差，亟需系统检验。

Method: 提出一个两阶段评估框架：第一阶段为校准实验，通过设计任务相关的测试样本来评估判别模型对任务的真实理解水平；第二阶段为敏感性实验，通过改变提示中是否包含参考答案及其位置，观察判别模型评分的动态变化，从而揭示参考信息对判别结果的显著影响。实验覆盖三种语言，确保结果具有跨语言泛化性。

Result: LLM判别器在无参考答案时普遍高估错误回答，而在引入参考答案后，其判断准确率出现大幅反转，最高可达85%的变化幅度。这一现象在不同语言中均被观察到，且其变化方向与人类评判基本一致，说明判别器的决策严重依赖于参考信息的存在。

Conclusion: LLM判别器在无参考设置下的评估表现不可靠，其判断高度受参考答案存在与否及位置的影响。因此，在实际应用前必须通过包含参考信息的样本进行校准，以确保其在无参考环境中的有效性。本研究提供了一套可推广的校准方法，有助于提升未来评估系统的可信度。

Abstract: LLM judges are increasingly being used to evaluate open-ended model responses, often in no-reference settings where a ground-truth answer is unavailable. However, can they reliably assess in such evaluation setups? We explore this question in this paper through a two stage pipeline with a) calibration experiments that assess the judge model's knowledge of the task it is evaluating, and b) sensitivity experiments that assess how the judge model's performance is impacted by the presence and positioning of the reference answer in the prompt. Across experiments covering three languages, we show that the judge models we evaluated tend to over-credit incorrect answers in the absence of a reference answer, and adding reference answer information to the prompt flips the judge model's correct/incorrect decisions by as much as 85% in some experimental settings. Comparison with a subset of human annotations shows that these reference-driven changes generally align with human judgments. Our results emphasize the need for calibrating the LLM judges with a sample with reference-aware evaluation before using them in reference-free setups reliably, and our methodology provides a blueprint for researchers and practitioners in doing such calibration of LLM judges for other tasks.

</details>


### [141] [The Illusion of Robustness: Aggregate Accuracy Hides Prediction Flips under Task-Irrelevant Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12963)
*Yanzhe Zhang,Sanmi Koyejo,Diyi Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 尽管最先进的大语言模型在整体上对无关上下文表现出鲁棒性，但其在单个样本上的预测却存在显著不稳定性。即使是无意义的伪词，也能显著改变部分样本的模型预测结果，且这种影响在不同模型间具有差异性。该现象受上下文类型、长度、推理时计算资源和模型发展阶段的影响，揭示了被平均准确率掩盖的上下文诱导的尾部风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在复杂上下文中部署日益广泛，但其对无关上下文的可靠性尚不明确。现有评估主要依赖于整体准确率，可能掩盖了模型在个别样本上的严重不稳定问题。因此需要更细致的评估方式以识别潜在风险。

Method: 通过在基准测试问题前添加长而无关的上下文（包括随机字符组成的伪词），系统地评估多个大语言模型在不同数据集上的表现变化。分析了模型预测在个体样本层面的波动情况，并考察了上下文类型、长度、计算资源和模型版本等因素的影响。

Result: 虽然整体准确率变化不大，但部分样本的预测结果受到显著影响：一些样本性能下降，另一些则提升。这种不稳定性普遍存在，但受影响的样本因模型而异，且受上下文特征和模型状态调节。

Conclusion: 聚合准确率无法反映模型在真实场景中的可靠性，尤其是在面对无关上下文时。应引入针对每个样本的可靠性评估机制，以识别并缓解由上下文引发的潜在风险。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) grow more capable, they are increasingly deployed in context-rich settings where task inputs are often accompanied by long, partially irrelevant context. In a controlled setting, we find that state-of-the-art models often appear robust to task-irrelevant context at the aggregate level: prepending it to benchmark questions causes little change in overall accuracy. This aggregate stability, however, masks significant per-example instability. Even semantically meaningless pseudo-words, formed by randomly combining characters, can markedly shift model predictions on a small fraction of examples, degrading performance on some while improving it on others. This two-sided effect holds consistently across a wide range of models and datasets, yet the affected examples are largely model-specific. We further show that this instability is modulated by context type, context length, test-time compute, and model development stage. Together, our findings reveal context-induced tail risks concealed by aggregate accuracy, motivating per-example reliability evaluation of language models.

</details>


### [142] [PalmClaw: A Native On-Device Agent Framework for Mobile Phones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13027)
*Hongru Cai,Yongqi Li,Ran Wei,Wenjie Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PalmClaw 是一个开源的移动端智能体框架，可在手机上原生运行，直接管理会话、记忆、技能、工具和智能体循环。它将设备功能暴露为具有明确参数、结构化结果和清晰执行边界的工具，使智能体能直接调用移动设备能力，同时保持每一步操作的透明与可控。实验表明，相比最强基线，任务成功率提升11.5%，完成时间减少94.9%，且设置负担更低，可清晰追踪执行边界的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有移动端智能体主要通过图形界面（GUI）操作（如点击、滑动）执行任务，这类方法依赖界面，难以直接访问设备能力，且执行边界模糊。为解决这些问题，需要一种能在手机上原生运行、直接利用设备能力并具备清晰控制机制的智能体框架。

Method: 提出 PalmClaw 框架，将设备功能抽象为结构化工具，支持在本地设备上直接调用，并设计了会话管理、记忆、技能和智能体循环机制，确保每一步操作都有明确输入、输出和执行边界。

Result: 在任务成功率上相对基线提升 11.5%，任务完成时间减少 94.9%，部署更简便，且能清晰展示执行边界的划分与应用。

Conclusion: PalmClaw 实现了在移动端原生运行的高效、可控智能体系统，通过将设备能力转化为结构化工具，显著提升了任务执行效率与可靠性，为移动智能体发展提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents have moved beyond generating responses to executing multi-step tasks by calling tools, observing the results, and iteratively deciding the next action. Most agent systems run on desktops or servers, which support tool use and task automation. Mobile devices are also important agent environments because they are widely accessible and contain users' data, sensors, and daily-use applications. Existing mobile agents mainly operate smartphones through graphical user interface (GUI) actions such as tapping, swiping, and typing, which often form long, interface-dependent sequences, cannot directly access device capabilities, and make execution boundaries difficult to define. We present \textbf{PalmClaw}, an open-source agent framework that runs natively on mobile phones and manages the sessions, memory, skills, tools, and agent loop directly on the device. PalmClaw exposes device capabilities as device tools with explicit arguments, structured results, and clearly defined execution boundaries. This design enables agents to use mobile capabilities directly while keeping each action explicit and controlled. Experiments show an 11.5\% relative improvement in task success and a 94.9\% reduction in completion time over the strongest baseline, with lower setup burden and traces illustrating how execution boundaries are applied. Code is available at https://github.com/ModalityDance/PalmClaw.

### [143] [OmniPMNet: Bridging discrete and gridded PM10 forecasts via omni-query neural processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11896)
*Shuangshuang He,Shuo Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OmniPM-Net 是一种基于 ConvCNP 的融合模型，结合了化学传输模型（CTMs）与图神经网络（GNNs）的优势，实现高精度的站点级预测和连续的网格化空间场输出。通过地形感知的高斯集合卷积将不规则站点预测上采样至规则网格，并利用多尺度空间源注意力模块融合 CAMS 信息，最终在 108 小时预报范围内生成一致的 PM10 预测结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法中，化学传输模型（CTMs）虽能提供连续的网格化预测但存在局部偏差；而图神经网络（GNNs）在短时站点预测上表现良好，但无法生成网格化输出。因此亟需一种能够同时兼顾站点精度与空间连续性的融合模型，尤其在严重沙尘暴期间更为关键。

Method: 提出 OmniPM-Net 模型，采用卷积条件神经过程（ConvCNP）框架，在共享空间表示下融合 GNN 站点预测与 CAMS 格网数据。引入地形感知的高斯集合卷积将不规则站点预测映射到规则网格，并设计多尺度空间源注意力（SSA）模块进行跨源信息融合；最后通过共享的全查询读出机制，统一生成站点或格网点上的预测结果。

Result: 在2024年中国1,618个空气质量监测站的全年评估中，OmniPM-Net 在站点层面的平均绝对误差为21.14 μg/m³，优于更强的GNN基线（22.00 μg/m³），且比CAMS降低30%的误差。在高浓度尾部（90百分位）误差下降9%（相对于GNN）和25%（相对于CAMS），在沙尘暴期间显著提升分类检测能力并准确追踪空间演变轨迹。

Conclusion: OmniPM-Net 成功实现了站点精度与空间连续性的统一，尤其在极端污染事件中表现突出，为高分辨率、高精度的颗粒物污染预报提供了新范式。

Abstract: Forecasting particulate matter (PM10) requires both station-scale accuracy and continuous spatial fields, especially during severe dust storms. Chemical transport models (CTMs) provide gridded forecasts but retain local biases, whereas graph neural networks (GNNs) track monitoring sites well at short lead times but do not produce gridded outputs. Here we present OmniPM-Net, a Convolutional Conditional Neural Process (ConvCNP)-based fusion model that reconciles these two forecast types within a shared spatial representation. A terrain-aware Gaussian set convolution lifts irregular GNN station forecasts onto a regular grid, where a multi-scale Spatial Source Attention (SSA) module blends them with Copernicus Atmosphere Monitoring Service (CAMS) forecasts; a shared omni-query readout then decodes this representation into consistent PM10 predictions at either stations or grid cells over a 108 h horizon. Evaluated across 1,618 air-quality monitoring stations throughout China over the full year of 2024, OmniPM-Net matches the station-level accuracy of the stronger GNN baseline (mean absolute error 21.14 versus 22.00 ug/m3) and reduces the CAMS mean absolute error by 30%, while simultaneously delivering the gridded fields that the discrete GNN cannot. Its clearest gains are in the high-concentration tail, where the 90th-percentile MAE falls by 9% relative to the GNN and 25% relative to CAMS, and during dust episodes, where it improves categorical detection skill while tracking the evolving spatial trajectory.

### [144] [Semidirect Fourier Delta Attention: Phase-Controlled Delta Memory with Constructive Chunk-WY Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11897)
*Tiantian Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为半直接傅里叶差分注意力（SFDA）的新方法，通过块旋转傅里叶控制替代传统的实对角衰减，实现相位可控的线性注意力机制。该方法基于构造性的分块-WY分解，保证了在固定块内秩增长受限，从而实现精确的仿射分块转移、形式稳定性与复杂度边界，并能紧凑表征相位加低秩记忆。数值验证和小规模状态追踪实验表明，SFDA能够学习周期性记忆，而相位禁用的基线方法表现接近随机水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有线性注意力机制由于使用固定递归状态压缩键值缓存，限制了精确的状态跟踪和长序列记忆能力。为解决这一问题，需要一种既能保持计算效率又能支持长期依赖建模的新型注意力结构。

Method: 引入半直接傅里叶差分注意力（SFDA），以复数域中的块旋转傅里叶矩阵作为相位控制机制，取代原有的实对角衰减。通过构造性地推导出分块-WY分解，将注意力更新表示为一个包含低秩修正项的乘积形式，确保在固定块内秩增长受控。

Result: 实现了精确的仿射分块转移，证明了算法的形式稳定性和复杂度上界；数值实验显示其可有效学习周期性记忆模式，显著优于相位缺失的基线模型（如KDA）。

Conclusion: SFDA提供了一种兼具高效性与强表达力的线性注意力框架，能够在不增加内存开销的前提下建模长程依赖与周期性动态，为大规模语言模型中的长上下文处理提供了理论基础与新思路。

Abstract: Linear attention replaces softmax attention's growing KV cache with a fixed recurrent state, but this compression limits exact state tracking and long-context memory. We introduce \emph{Semidirect Fourier Delta Attention} (SFDA), a phase-controlled generalization of Kimi Delta Attention that replaces real diagonal decay with block-rotational Fourier control: \[ S_t=(I-β_t k_tk_t^*)Λ_tS_{t-1}+β_tk_tv_t^*, \qquad Λ_t=\diag(α_t\odot e^{iθ_t}). \] Our main result is a constructive chunk-WY factorization for products \(A_t=Λ_t-u_tr_t^*\), giving \[ A_t\cdots A_1=Γ_t-Y_tM_tW_t^* \] with rank growth bounded inside fixed chunks. This yields an exact affine chunk transfer, formal stability and complexity bounds, and a compact characterization of phase-plus-low-rank memory. We verify the algebra numerically and show in toy state-tracking experiments that SFDA learns cyclic memory where the phase-disabled KDA baseline remains near chance. Fused kernels and large-scale language-model comparisons are left to future work.

</details>


### [145] [Repairing Shape-Prior Shortcuts in Long-Range Single-Shot Fringe Projection Profilometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11928)
*Adam Haroon,Cody Fleming,Beiwen Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PhiCalNet 是一种新型单帧相位投影轮廓术（FPP）网络，通过输出包裹相位表示（sinφ, cosφ）并利用固定可微校准层映射到深度，从架构上消除形状先验捷径。相比传统 UNet 基线（MAE 14.54 mm），PhiCalNet 将物体平均绝对误差降低至 4.46 mm，且在 ±π 包裹不连续处仅 0.103% 的像素存在残差；三帧扩展进一步降至 1.16 mm。通过可解释性分析和像素级共形不确定性量化验证，相位是最佳可解内部特征，且错误集中于包裹不连续区域，剔除顶部 5% 不一致像素可使均方根误差下降 64%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单帧 FPP 网络因直接回归深度而依赖形状先验，仅从边界恢复深度而非真实相位，导致性能受限；即使增加数据或模型容量也无法突破该瓶颈，因为优化器仍在相同假设空间中搜索。因此需要从根本上改变网络架构以避免该捷径。

Method: 提出 PhiCalNet，其输出为包裹相位的正弦与余弦表示 (sinφ, cosφ)，并通过一个固定、可微的校准层将相位映射至深度。引入额外的条纹序号作为辅助输入以解决单帧映射非单射问题。采用物理信息神经网络（PINN）基线对比，证明架构选择才是关键因素而非损失函数设计。

Result: PhiCalNet 在合成基准上将物体平均绝对误差（MAE）从 14.54 mm 降至 4.46 mm，显著优于传统方法；其残差主要集中在 ±π 包裹不连续点，占比仅 0.103%；三帧扩展版本达到 1.16 mm；像素级不确定性量化首次应用于 FPP，有效定位错误区域，剔除 5% 最不确定像素后，误差下降 64%。

Conclusion: 通过架构设计主动排除形状先验捷径，使相位成为可解内部表示，是提升单帧 FPP 性能的关键。该方法不仅大幅提高精度，还提供了可解释性和不确定性量化能力，为未来高精度三维重建提供新范式。

Abstract: Single-shot fringe projection profilometry (FPP) networks that regress depth directly can exploit a shape-prior shortcut, recovering depth from object boundaries rather than from fringe phase. On a photorealistic synthetic benchmark (15,600 fringe images, 50 objects at 1.5-2.1 m standoff), the best such UNet baseline plateaus at 14.54 mm object mean absolute error (MAE), and neither more data nor more capacity removes the shortcut, because neither changes the hypothesis space the optimizer searches. We introduce PhiCalNet, which outputs a wrapped-phase representation $(\sinφ, \cosφ)$ and maps it to depth through a fixed differentiable calibration layer, removing the shape-prior solution architecturally rather than by a loss penalty. Because the single-shot mapping is non-injective without fringe order, PhiCalNet takes the fringe order as auxiliary input, an assumption a sensitivity analysis shows tolerates realistic decoding error; a physics-informed (PINN) baseline with the same physics as a soft penalty yields no gain, isolating the architectural choice as the operative factor. PhiCalNet reduces object MAE 3.3x to 4.46 mm, its residual confined to 0.103% of pixels at the $\pmπ$ wrap discontinuity, and a three-frame extension reaches 1.16 mm. Two checks agree: interpretability makes phase the most decodable internal feature, and pixel-wise conformal uncertainty quantification, to our knowledge the first for FPP, localizes error at the same discontinuity, where rejecting the top 5% of pixels by snapshot disagreement cuts root-mean-square error by 64% versus 3.5% for the baseline.

</details>


### [146] [Qubit-Efficient Quantum Search for Hyperdimensional Decomposition via Logarithmic Encoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11936)
*Sanggeon Yun,Hyunwoo Oh,Ryozo Masukawa,Raheeb Hassan,Mohsen Imani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种量子高效框架，用于高维计算（HDC）中的超向量分解，将表示成本从O(D)降低到O(log D)，通过引入对数超向量和绑定编码，结合可逆超向量查找算子与改进的Dürr-Høyer搜索算法，在保持O(√(N^F))搜索复杂度的同时显著减少量子比特使用，实验验证了其在相似性计算和分解准确性方面的有效性，并实现最多2000倍的量子比特节省。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超向量分解面临计算瓶颈，需在N^F个候选组合中搜索，且现有量子方法依赖于高成本的O(D)量子比特表示，限制了大规模应用。因此需要一种更高效的量子表示与搜索机制以提升可扩展性。

Method: 提出对数超向量与绑定编码，设计可逆超向量查找算子，结合改进的Dürr-Høyer搜索过程，实现低量子比特开销下的高效搜索。

Result: 实验表明该方法能正确进行相似性计算，实现在可执行范围内的准确分解，相比基于显式D-量子比特表示的基线方法，量子比特使用减少达2000倍。

Conclusion: 所提出的量子高效框架有效降低了超向量分解的资源需求，同时保持了原有的搜索优势，为大规模高维计算的量子实现提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Hyperdimensional Computing (HDC) represents symbols using high-dimensional hypervectors of dimension $D$. In hypervector decomposition, the objective is to recover $F$ constituent hypervectors, each drawn from a codebook of size $N$, from a bound target hypervector. This requires searching over $N^F$ candidate tuples, making the task computationally prohibitive at scale. Recent quantum approach provides a quadratic search advantage, but typically rely on qubit-inefficient $O(D)$-qubit hypervector representations. We propose a qubit-efficient quantum framework for HDC decomposition that reduces the representation cost to $O(\log D)$. The framework introduces logarithmic hypervector and binding encodings, together with a reversible hypervector lookup operator for circuit-level manipulation of dense hypervectors. Combined with a modified Dürr-Høyer search procedure, the method preserves $O(\sqrt{N^F})$ search complexity while substantially reducing qubit usage. Experimental results validate correct similarity computation, accurate decomposition in executable regimes, and significantly improved qubit scaling over baselines based on explicit $D$-qubit hypervector encodings, achieving up to $2{,}000\times$ fewer qubits.

### [147] [Mirror Horizon: Viable Path Entropy as a Measure of Bounded Reflection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11937)
*Tiantian Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Mirror Theory introduces viable path entropy (VPE) to measure an intelligent system's capacity for sustained, verified continuations under reflection. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To develop a more comprehensive measure of intelligence beyond static representation or one-shot performance, by focusing on the system's ability to sustain coherent, verified continuations through repeated reflection.

Method: Introduce viable path entropy (VPE) as a finite-budget measure combining reachability probability and verified-mode diversity; apply it to language model reasoning via rollout protocols with verifiers and mode maps across different reflection horizons and token budgets.

Result: Increasing token budget from 96 to 160 significantly improves verified reachability, reduces zero-reachability, increases verified-mode entropy, and boosts smoothed VPE. Qwen2.5-1.5B achieves the strongest mirror horizon despite having fewer parameters than Qwen2.5-3B, indicating that mirror horizon depends on accessible verified continuation capacity rather than model size.

Abstract: Mirror Theory proposes that an intelligent system should be studied not only by what it represents, but by what coherent continuations it can sustain under repeated reflection. We make this claim operational through \emph{viable path entropy} (VPE), a finite-budget measure of verified continuation capacity. Given a mirror state, a rollout protocol, a verifier, and a mode map, VPE decomposes bounded capability into two parts: the probability of reaching a viable continuation and the diversity of verified continuation modes reached among successful rollouts. This paper restores the full theoretical scaffold behind the measure: intuition as local underdetermining constraint, taste as invariant-selecting pressure, reflection as taste-guided resolution of underdetermination, and geometry as the learned structure that makes future reflection stable. We then instantiate the theory in language-model reasoning experiments on GSM8K. Across Qwen2.5-Instruct models, 32 sampled rollouts per problem, and two reflection horizons, increasing the token budget from 96 to 160 substantially expands verified reachability, reduces zero-reachability, increases verified-mode entropy, and improves smoothed VPE. At 160 tokens, Qwen2.5-1.5B realizes the strongest mirror horizon among the tested models, even though Qwen2.5-3B has more parameters. This shows that mirror horizon is not parameter count, but accessible verified continuation capacity under a bounded reflection protocol. The result supports Mirror Theory as a measure-level account: capability is the structure of viable continuations made reachable, not merely one-shot accuracy or pass@k.

### [149] [CARE-LoRA: Compressed Activation REconstruction for Memory-Efficient LoRA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11940)
*Gengyu Zhang,Haiyin Ran,Zhengbao He,Yuhang Liu,Hanling Tian,Zhehao Huang,Xiaolin Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CARE-LoRA 是一种数据感知的压缩激活重建框架，旨在解决低秩适应（LoRA）微调中的内存瓶颈问题。通过利用 LoRA 的投影结构，将完整的输入激活替换为低秩压缩激活，并在前向传播中计算轻量级重建矩阵，以在反向传播中重建梯度信号，从而保持 LoRA 矩阵的完全可训练性。实验表明，CARE-LoRA 在显著降低内存占用的同时，性能优于或媲美标准 LoRA 及其他变体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模预训练模型微调过程中，尽管 LoRA 通过仅优化低秩矩阵减少了参数量，但保留用于反向传播的激活仍构成主要内存瓶颈，亟需有效解决方案。

Method: CARE-LoRA 利用 LoRA 的投影结构，将输入激活压缩为低秩形式，通过前向传播生成轻量级重建矩阵，在反向传播中用于梯度信号重建，实现内存高效且保持可训练性。

Result: CARE-LoRA 显著降低了整体内存开销，同时在多种模型和下游任务上实现了与标准 LoRA 或更优的性能表现。

Conclusion: CARE-LoRA 有效缓解了 LoRA 微调中的激活内存瓶颈，是一种高效、可扩展的参数高效微调方法，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: As the scale of large pre-trained models continues to grow, fine-tuning them under limited memory budgets has become increasingly challenging. Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), currently one of the most widely adopted parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) methods, mitigates this challenge by optimizing only low-rank adaptation matrices, thereby greatly reducing the number of trainable parameters. With the parameter overhead substantially reduced, the activations retained for backpropagation have emerged as the primary remaining memory bottleneck during LoRA fine-tuning. To address this, we propose CARE-LoRA, a data-aware Compressed Activation REconstruction framework. By exploiting the inherent projection structure of LoRA, CARE-LoRA replaces the full input activation with the low-rank compressed activation naturally produced by the LoRA branch. It further computes a lightweight reconstruction matrix during the forward pass with negligible additional computation cost, which is used during backpropagation to reconstruct the gradient signal, thereby keeping LoRA matrices fully trainable. Extensive experiments across diverse models and downstream tasks demonstrate that, while substantially reducing the overall memory footprint, CARE-LoRA achieves competitive or even superior performance compared with standard LoRA and representative LoRA variants. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/fishandyu/CARE-LoRA .

### [150] [How Query Visibility Changes KV-Cache Compression Rankings: A Matched-Budget Audit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11942)
*Daming Luo,Christy Liang,Junyu Xuan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究对六种已发表的KV缓存压缩方法在三种开放7-9B模型上进行了匹配预算审计，对比了三种简单基线方法。实验采用查询无关（query-agnostic）协议，即在未见查询时进行压缩，以评估其在真实场景中的可重用性。结果表明：(1) 查询可见性显著改变压缩方法的排名；在查询无关协议下，仅KeyDiff在36个测试单元中持续优于最佳基线（31次），而广泛使用的SnapKV平均表现低于‘保留开头和最近窗口’基线（-0.066）；(2) 各方法在两种协议间的性能下降幅度与其评分信号对查询的依赖程度一致：从SnapKV（Δ=+0.198，查询在其64词观察窗口内）到KeyDiff（Δ=+0.011，评分不含查询信息）呈递减趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV缓存压缩方法多在查询可见的条件下评估（查询感知协议），但实际应用中更关键的是压缩后可多次重用——即在无查询前提下进行压缩。因此，需要在查询无关条件下重新评估这些方法的有效性，以揭示其真实部署潜力。

Method: 在三个公开的7-9B模型上，对六种压缩方法与三种基线进行大规模配对评估（共144,300次在RULER-8192上，40,800次在LongBench上，50,000次重采样自助法）。所有条件保持一致，仅改变评分规则（查询感知 vs. 查询无关），通过对比不同协议下的性能变化，分析方法对查询的依赖性。

Result: 1. 在查询无关协议下，仅有KeyDiff持续优于最佳基线（31/36单元）；SnapKV平均表现劣于简单基线（-0.066）；2. 各方法在两种协议间的性能差异与其评分信号对查询的敏感度严格对应：依赖查询越强，性能下降越大，体现于源码逻辑中。

Conclusion: 当前主流的KV缓存压缩方法在真实可重用场景中表现不佳，其性能高度依赖查询可见性。未来设计应转向不依赖查询的评分机制，以实现真正意义上的高效、通用压缩。

Abstract: KV-cache compression methods are predominantly evaluated with the query appended to the context before compression -- a query-aware protocol. Yet the economic case for a compressed KV cache is reuse: compress a document once, answer many future questions against it. In that deployment, compression must happen query-agnostic -- before any question is seen. We present a matched-budget audit of six published compression methods against three trivial baselines on three open 7-9B models (144,300 paired evaluations on RULER-8192; 40,800 on LongBench; 50,000-resample paired bootstrap throughout). Everything is held fixed -- model, compression ratio, instances, decoding -- except the scoring rule. Three findings. (1) Query visibility changes the rankings: under the agnostic protocol, of the five audited methods that share a common attention backend, only KeyDiff beats a best-of-3 trivial baseline consistently (31 of 36 cells), and the most widely deployed method, SnapKV, loses to "keep the start and the recent window" on average (-0.066). (2) The per-method drop between the two protocols is ordered consistently with how visible the question is to each method's scoring signal, legible in its source code: from Delta=+0.198 for SnapKV (the question sits inside its 64-token observation window) down to Delta=+0.011 for KeyDiff (its score contains no query term at all).

Abstract: Long-horizon physics-based simulations of battery degradation provide mechanistic insight but remain computationally expensive, limiting their use for dense exploration of operating conditions over extended cycle life. Here, we propose a hybrid physics-probabilistic learning framework for surrogate modeling of lithium-ion battery degradation trajectories at unseen charging rates. Cycle-resolved degradation data generated with a DFN/P2D electrochemical model in PyBaMM are first transformed into capacity-aligned voltage and derivative features and encoded using a Variational Autoencoder (VAE). The resulting two-dimensional latent space organizes degradation trajectories according to both cycle progression and charging protocol. A sparse multitask Gaussian process (GP) is then trained in this latent space using cycle number and C-rate as input variables, providing continuous interpolation of latent degradation dynamics together with posterior uncertainty estimates. Under protocol-level holdout evaluation, the latent-space GP accurately recovers unseen C-rate trajectories and exhibits uncertainty behavior consistent with the support of the training data. When queried at unseen interior C-rates, the model generates latent trajectories that remain coherently positioned between neighboring simulated protocols. Decoding the GP-predicted latent states through the frozen VAE decoder yields smooth voltage-capacity evolution, while Monte Carlo propagation of the GP latent posterior through an auxiliary latent to State of Health (SOH) predictor provides uncertainty-aware SOH estimates. The proposed BattVAE-GP framework therefore offers a computationally efficient and uncertainty-aware surrogate for long-horizon degradation modeling, providing a structured basis for extending battery health prediction toward richer operating conditions and future simulation-experiment fusion.

### [153] [Scale-Aware Attention for Scarce Neural Data: An RG-Flow Transformer on Sleep-EDF EEG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11950)

Abstract: Brain field potentials are scale-free: their power spectra follow a $1/f^β$ law whose aperiodic exponent $β$ tracks cortical state, and sleep depth in particular is a shift in $β$. Across $5$ subjects and $5$ seeds under leave-one-subject-out cross-validation, RG-Flow and the vanilla transformer are statistically indistinguishable on 5-class staging (77.3\% vs 77.0\% accuracy; paired $p=0.294$), and the predicted scarce-data crossover does not appear: vanilla is numerically ahead at every data-limited budget. What does separate the models is interpretability -- RG-Flow recovers the continuous spectral exponent out-of-sample ($β$-recovery $R^2 = 0.416$), a capability the vanilla architecture has no analogue for.

*Elaheh Hassani,Durga Mandarapu,Qi Yu,Hanghang Tong,Ariful Azad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FastAlign 是一种可扩展的、感知稀疏性的框架，用于基于最优传输的网络对齐。它通过将原始最优传输计算重新解释为一系列重复的混合稀疏-密集操作，保留了原有的OT公式，同时结合稀疏感知图计算与领域特定的内核融合（如自定义SpMM内核），在不牺牲对齐精度的前提下显著提升了效率。实验表明，FastAlign 在CPU上将端到端运行时间减少了3.89x–9.45x，在GPU上减少了2.24x–32.54x，对齐质量与现有最优方法相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于最优传输的网络对齐方法虽然精度高，但频繁构建和更新稠密矩阵导致可扩展性差。需要在保持高对齐精度的同时提升计算效率，尤其针对大规模网络场景。

Method: FastAlign 将原始最优传输计算重新表述为一系列混合稀疏-密集操作，利用稀疏感知图计算技术，并引入领域特定的内核融合策略，包括自定义SpMM（稀疏矩阵-稠密矩阵乘法）内核，以优化计算性能。

Result: FastAlign 在保持与现有最优OT方法相当对齐质量的前提下，显著降低了计算时间：在CPU上加速3.89x–9.45x，GPU上加速2.24x–32.54x。

Conclusion: FastAlign 有效解决了现有最优传输方法在大规模网络对齐中的可扩展性瓶颈，实现了高精度与高性能的平衡，适用于实际大规模数据场景。

Abstract: Network alignment identifies node correspondences across different networks and is a fundamental primitive in many data science applications, including social network analysis, fraud detection, and knowledge graph integration. However, state-of-the-art network alignment methods often achieve high accuracy by repeatedly constructing and updating dense matrices, sacrificing scalability in the process. To address this scalability limitation without compromising alignment accuracy, we present FastAlign, a scalable, sparsity-aware framework for optimal transport-based network alignment. Rather than introducing a new alignment model, FastAlign preserves the original OT formulation and reinterprets its computation as a set of recurring mixed sparse-dense operations. FastAlign combines sparsity-aware graph computation with domain-specific kernel fusion, including a custom SpMM kernel. Our results show that FastAlign achieves alignment quality comparable to state-of-the-art OT-based methods while substantially reducing end-to-end runtime up to 3.89x-9.45x on CPU and 2.24x-32.54x on GPU.

</details>


### [155] [When Does Reward Teach State? A Hidden-Automaton Instrument and the Group-Language Boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11953)
*Jim Allchin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过将任务建模为隐藏的确定性有限自动机（DFA），提出了一种可精确回答“强化学习代理是否真正理解任务潜在状态”的白盒方法。研究分离了奖励成功与状态学习两个指标，通过控制优化器强度、任务结构和观察信息量三个维度，发现高奖励不等于状态理解；感知差距（状态不可线性恢复）与规划差距（状态可恢复但未使用）可被区分。即使在稀疏奖励下，通过合适的算法（如PPO+GAE）仍可部分恢复状态，且任务结构可提前预测感知缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统强化学习中，任务的‘真实状态’常无法定义，导致难以判断代理是否真正理解任务。本研究旨在建立一个可精确评估代理对任务潜在状态理解程度的框架，以解决奖励成功与状态学习之间的混淆问题。

Method: 将任务建模为隐藏的确定性有限自动机（DFA），让代理基于符号流进行决策，并在稀疏奖励下完成接受状态判定。利用已知的自动机结构，可精确计算最优回报并获取每一步的真实状态，从而直接评估代理的状态表示能力。通过调节优化器强度、任务结构（如排列语言结构）和观察信息量，系统分析状态学习与奖励表现的关系。

Result: 1. 弱策略梯度方法下，代理状态探测仅达到随机水平，表明稀疏奖励可能无法建立状态表示；2. 但在预注册控制实验中，PPO+GAE能部分恢复状态，但存在高种子方差；3. 任务的排列结构可作为感知缺口的预警信号，提前预测状态不可恢复性，准确率达86%（89/103）；4. 观察信息越丰富，辅助任务越有效，揭示了感知与规划两类差距的区别。

Conclusion: 高奖励不能作为代理理解任务的证据；其是否掌握潜在状态可通过任务结构、观察质量及优化器设计提前预测。该研究为评估代理认知深度提供了可量化的工具，突破了传统奖励导向评价的局限。

Abstract: Does a reinforcement-learning agent that earns high reward represent its task's latent state, or only a reward-correlated shortcut? The question is usually unanswerable: the "true state" is undefined. We make it exactly answerable with a white-box instrument: express the task as a hidden deterministic finite automaton (DFA), let the agent observe a symbol stream and intermittently choose the next symbol under partial control, and grant one sparse terminal reward for acceptance. Knowing the automaton gives two things for free: the optimal return (so reward becomes an interpretable normalized score) and the exact latent state at every step (so we can probe the agent's representation without ever showing it). Reward success and latent-state learning thus become separately measured quantities whose coupling is governed by three controllable axes. Optimizer strength: under weak on-policy RL the agent earns reward with the state probe at chance for every architecture, tempting the conclusion that sparse RL cannot install latent state; a pre-registered control overturns it -- PPO+GAE recovers the state, but only partially and with high seed variance. Task structure: permutation (group-language) structure is a warning sign computable from the transition function before any training, and held out on 153 capacity-controlled fresh automata it flags perception gaps at precision 0.86 (89 of 103), in one direction only. Observation informativeness: a label-free auxiliary is vacuous when observations carry no state and recovers it in proportion to how much they reveal. The payoff is a distinction reward-only evaluation cannot make: a perception gap (latent state not linearly recoverable, though representable) versus a planning gap (state recoverable but unused). High reward is thus not evidence of task understanding; whether an agent recovers latent state is predictable in advance.

</details>


### [156] [Graph-Constrained Policy Learning for Extreme Clinical Code Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11954)
*Amritpal Singh,Sebastian Torres,Khawar Shakeel,Syed Ahmad Chan Bukhari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种图约束遍历策略，将临床代码预测建模为在修剪后的代码层级图上的有限时域决策过程。通过单一语言模型逐层下降，选择有效子节点直至达到可计费的叶节点代码，从而将极端多标签预测转化为稀疏、层次感知的子集决策，保证输出结构有效性。在MIMIC-IV数据集上，该方法在50个代码子集和完整15,761个代码空间中分别取得0.709和0.527的micro-F1，优于现有扁平化基线方法。实验表明，增加监督轨迹数据是唯一能持续提升性能的方法，而强化学习并未带来优势。结果表明，简单的图约束策略在极端临床编码预测任务中优于更复杂的扁平化、级联式及强化学习方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有临床代码预测系统通常将任务视为扁平多标签分类，独立评分代码，导致对罕见标签的训练信号不足。由于ICD-10-CM具有深层稀疏的层级结构，这种处理方式难以捕捉语义依赖关系并加剧了罕见代码的预测瓶颈。因此，需要一种能够利用层级结构、增强稀疏标签学习能力的新方法。

Method: 提出图约束遍历策略，将代码预测建模为在预处理过的代码层级图上的有限步决策过程。使用单一语言模型从根节点开始逐层选择合法子节点，直到到达叶节点代码。通过图剪枝减少搜索空间，确保生成的代码组合符合标准层级结构。采用监督微调（SFT）训练策略，构建轨迹数据以指导模型学习有效路径。

Result: 在MIMIC-IV数据集上，提出的SFT-1+模型在50代码子集上达到0.709 micro-F1，在完整15,761代码空间上达到0.527 micro-F1，显著优于CAM、LAAT、PLM-ICD等扁平基线模型。在全规模设置下，相比最强基线，micro-F1提升0.044，macro-F1提升0.157。控制因子实验显示，仅增加监督轨迹数据能稳定提升性能，强化学习未带来改进。单个共享策略即可媲美三阶段专家级联系统，且避免了上下文窗口溢出问题。

Conclusion: 图约束遍历策略通过结构化层级分解有效缓解了极端多标签临床代码预测中的罕见标签瓶颈。相比于复杂架构与强化学习方法，简单而有效的监督式图遍历策略表现更优，证明了在医疗文本理解中利用领域知识图谱进行结构引导建模的有效性。

Abstract: Clinical code prediction maps unstructured discharge summaries to ICD-10-CM leaf codes in a large, sparse, and deeply hierarchical label space. Most systems treat the task as flat multi-label classification, scoring codes independently and providing limited training signal for rare labels. We propose a graph-constrained traversal policy that formulates ICD prediction as a finite-horizon decision process over a pruned code hierarchy. A single language model descends the graph level by level, selecting valid child nodes until billable leaf codes are reached. This converts extreme multi-label prediction into sparse, hierarchy-aware subset decisions while guaranteeing structurally valid outputs.
  On MIMIC-IV discharge summaries, our best supervised policy, SFT-1+, achieves 0.709 micro-F1 on a curated 50-code subset and 0.527 micro-F1 on the full 15,761-code space, outperforming flat baselines including CAML, LAAT, and PLM-ICD. In the full setting, SFT-1+ improves over the strongest flat baseline by 0.044 micro-F1 and 0.157 macro-F1, suggesting that graph-constrained decomposition mitigates the rare-code bottleneck. A controlled factorial study evaluates architecture, training algorithm, and data budget. Across both scales, one shared policy matches a three-specialist cascade while avoiding its context-window overflow on 28-32% of full-space test notes. Increasing supervised trajectory data is the only intervention that consistently improves performance, while GRPO reinforcement learning provides no benefit over supervised continuation with matched data. These results show that simple graph-constrained policy learning can outperform more complex flat, cascaded, and reinforcement-learning alternatives for extreme clinical code prediction.

### [157] [Exact and Certified Data Shapley for Weighted k-Nearest-Neighbor Regression and Soft-Label Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11956)
*Zongye Lyu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了加权KNN回归数据Shapley的首个精确算法，解决了长期存在的计算难题。该方法基于动态规划，在固定精度下实现伪多项式时间复杂度，并通过12,716个对抗样本验证了零误差；同时提供了连续权重和目标值的可认证近似方案，具备机器可验证的误差保证。研究还揭示了问题的复杂性下界和访问模型的计算困难性，并扩展至多分类软标签场景。作者开源了首个精确的加权回归数据Shapley基准库，实验证明其结果与蒙特卡洛方法在统计上等价，但具有确定性、误差可证和审计参考价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据Shapley方法在加权KNN回归和软标签预测中缺乏精确算法，仅有的暴力解法时间复杂度为O(N^K)，难以实用。核心障碍在于加权回归预测为两个依赖联盟的求和之比，破坏了传统算法所依赖的可加性、阈值性和重复性结构。

Method: 提出一种基于联合整数状态（权重和、权重乘以标签和）的计数型动态规划算法，用于精确计算加权KNN回归数据Shapley；设计可认证的全息近似算法（FPTAS），提供每项输出的误差证书；建立复杂性理论下界与访问模型的硬性结果；扩展至多分类软标签情形。

Result: 成功实现加权KNN回归数据Shapley的伪多项式时间精确计算，验证无误；获得可认证的近似算法，86,400次检查未违反误差界限；证明了Ω(D_w)输出大小的下界及访问模型的计算难度；开源首个精确加权回归数据Shapley基准库；实验证明精确值与蒙特卡洛方法在统计上等价，但前者在排名一致性、确定性和审计方面具有显著优势。

Conclusion: 本工作首次实现了加权KNN回归数据Shapley的精确高效计算，填补了理论与实践之间的空白。所提出的算法不仅具备理论保障，且在实际任务中表现优异，为数据价值评估提供了可靠基准，推动了可信机器学习中的公平性与可解释性研究。

Abstract: Data Shapley is the standard principled answer to which training points are worth what, and its k-nearest-neighbor (KNN) specialization is the version deployed in practice: the exact estimator shipped by toolkits such as pyDVL and OpenDataVal. Exact algorithms are known for unweighted KNN and for weighted KNN classification, but weighted KNN regression and soft-label prediction have resisted: the only exact method is an O(N^K) brute force, exponential in neighborhood size K. The obstruction: the weighted regression prediction is a ratio of two coalition-dependent sums, whose normalization denominator breaks the additive, threshold, and duplication structures the prior polynomial algorithms rely on. We close this gap. We give (i) the first pseudo-polynomial-time exact algorithm (polynomial in N and K at fixed lattice precision) for weighted KNN-regression Data Shapley, a counting dynamic program over the joint integer state (sum of w, sum of w*y), verified against exhaustive enumeration with zero mismatch on 12,716 adversarial instances; (ii) a certified FPTAS for continuous weights and targets, with a machine-checkable per-value error certificate never violated across 86,400 checks; (iii) a complexity landscape, including an unconditional Omega(D_w) output-size lower bound and access-model hardness results; and (iv) a weighted soft-label multi-class extension. We release an open-source, CPU-only library and the first exact weighted-regression Data Shapley ground truth. On downstream mislabel detection our exact values are statistically equivalent to Monte-Carlo Data Shapley (dataset-level TOST, n=8, p<10^-4), the pre-registered outcome; the value of exactness is instead determinism, a certified error bound, and an exact reference for auditing estimators: Monte-Carlo did not reproduce the exact top-10% ranking at any budget tested, up to 3,000 permutations (~1.28e6 utility evaluations).

### [158] [Constructed Reality, Contested Priors: Decoupling and the Architecture of Cognitive Relapse Under the Free Energy Principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11958)
*MD Ibrahim Hossain Ridoy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨在自由能原理框架下，预测系统是否可能因合成环境的足够一致性而永久将该环境视为默认假设（即发生本体论反转）。通过使用卷积变分自编码器与循环潜在预测器的代理模型，研究发现尽管系统的表征能力保持稳定（准确率0.97-0.998），其默认行为却随混合流中基线内容比例r的变化而大幅波动，显示出学习与接受之间的解耦。尤其在中间r值时出现‘认知倒退’现象——系统输出先趋近目标域，后部分回退至基线域，表明对现实采纳的抵抗是结构性而非学习速度所致，为该现象提供了计算上的存在证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究预测系统是否能在合成环境中永久取代真实世界作为其默认假设（本体论反转），由于神经系统的实验不可行，需借助计算模型进行验证。

Method: 采用卷积变分自编码器与循环潜在预测器构成的代理系统，训练过程分为两阶段：先在基线视觉域上训练，再在混合流中引入不同比例的基线内容（由参数r控制）以模拟过渡。通过追踪表征能力（可区分性）与默认行为（无约束生成）的动态变化，分析二者是否解耦。

Result: 在90次重复实验中，表征准确性始终维持在高水准（0.97–0.998），不受r影响；而默认行为则随r显著变化，呈现从目标域向基线域的部分回退，形成‘认知倒退’现象。表明学习与接受机制存在根本性解耦，且对现实采纳的抵抗具有结构性特征。

Conclusion: 对现实采纳的抵抗并非源于学习速度，而是系统内在结构属性，本研究通过计算模型提供了该现象的存在性证明，揭示了预测系统在面对环境变化时的深层非线性行为模式。

Abstract: Under the free energy principle, a predictive system does not observe reality directly; it maintains a generative model of the world and experiences that model's best current hypothesis. Can a synthetic environment be made consistent enough that a predictive system's own inference machinery adopts it as this default hypothesis, permanently displacing the environment that first shaped it? We call this state ontological inversion. Because inducing and monitoring such a transition in a nervous system is neither ethical nor technically feasible, we study the underlying computational problem through a controlled proxy: a convolutional variational autoencoder paired with a recurrent latent predictor, whose evidence lower bound objective is mathematically identical, up to sign, to variational free energy itself. The network is trained first on a baseline visual domain, then on a mixed stream in which a swept rehearsal ratio r controls how much baseline content persists during transition to a target domain. Representational capacity, what the latent space can discriminate, is tracked separately from default behavior, what the system generates when left unconstrained. Across a full sweep of 90 runs, the two diverge sharply: representational accuracy stays near ceiling, 0.97 to 0.998, regardless of r, while default behavior spans nearly the system's entire range depending on r alone, a decoupling of learning from acceptance. More strikingly, at intermediate r the system's default output rises toward the target domain, then partially reverts toward the baseline while training continues unchanged, a structural failure we term cognitive relapse. Resistance to reality-adoption is not reducible to learning speed; it is a structural property with its own distinct failure modes, established here as a computational existence proof and nothing further.

</details>


### [159] [Evaluating Reliability in Machine Learning Models for Early Chronic Kidney Disease Prediction: A Systematic Review of Data Leakage and Predictor Stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11963)
*Mashrul Hossain,Nafesa Kibria,Fahim Shahriar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用系统性文献检索筛选出19项相关研究，构建信息泄露的结构化分类体系与量化评分框架，结合性能表现与特征稳定性分析评估研究可靠性。

Conclusion: 多数报告的性能提升并非源于真正的预测能力，而是由方法学缺陷如数据泄露所致，强调需加强方法学严谨性以提升研究可信度。

Abstract: The early detection of Chronic Kidney Disease using machine learning has attracted significant interest in healthcare-related computer science. Despite rapid advancements in this field, many reported studies remain inconsistent and potentially misleading. A significant drawback is the lack of organized evaluation regarding methodological concerns. Key issues include data leakage, limited access to temporal patient records and inconsistency in reported clinical indicators. This research offers a systematic literature review of existing CKD prediction studies using interpretable machine learning techniques, where nineteen relevant studies were selected via systematic searches across major academic databases. To assess methodological reliability, this study introduces a structured taxonomy of information leakage and a quantitative leakage scoring framework to systematically evaluate reliability across CKD prediction studies. The analysis reveals a strong relationship between leakage and inflated performance. Here, High leakage-studies report an average accuracy of 95.48%, compared to 80.2% for leakage-free studies, reflecting an increase of approximately 15.28%. Furthermore, a cross-study feature stability analysis shows that only a small subset of predictors is consistently reproducible, with over 80% lacking reliability. Overall, the findings suggest that many reported performance improvements stem from methodological limitations rather than true predictive capability.

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LIDAR-AD提出一种无需解码器的潜空间交互梦想者框架，通过减少冗余信息并聚焦风险相关关系，改进自动驾驶中的长时程决策。它采用残差动作更新和对比学习来建模连续控制，并在潜空间中实现平滑、紧凑的动作调整。该方法在多个模拟场景中表现优异，显著提升奖励与成功率，且在真实交通布局下具有良好的可迁移性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于潜空间的世界模型在自动驾驶中因多源观测包含无关控制的冗余信息，导致观察重建和绝对动作建模不理想，难以捕捉决策相关的动态变化。因此需要更高效地提取风险相关特征并精确建模连续控制行为。

Method: LIDAR-AD采用无解码器设计，以冗余减少的潜空间对齐替代观察重建；将车辆控制建模为残差动作更新，并使用残差动作序列对比学习对齐多步滚动预测与未来状态；利用潜空间-tanh残差参数化保证动作可达性的同时实现长时程平滑控制。

Result: 在多种模拟驾驶场景中，LIDAR-AD显著优于基线世界模型，获得最高奖励和最佳成功率；在nuPlan重构的真实场景中也展现出强泛化能力，验证其在真实交通环境下的适用性。

Conclusion: LIDAR-AD通过聚焦风险相关关系、优化连续控制建模和提升长时程动态预测能力，有效解决了自动驾驶中潜空间决策建模的挑战，具备高度实用性和可迁移性。

Abstract: Autonomous driving requires long-horizon closedloop decision making in dynamic traffic environments. Latent world models offer an effective framework for this problem by enabling imagination-based decision making in compact latent spaces. However, multi-source observations contain controlirrelevant redundancy, whereas reliable driving decisions rely on risk-relevant relations, future dynamics, and continuous action adjustments. This mismatch makes observation reconstruction and absolute action modeling suboptimal for learning decisionrelevant latent dynamics. We propose LIDAR-AD, a decoderfree Latent-Interaction Dreamer with Action-Residual Chains for autonomous driving. LIDAR-AD replaces observation reconstruction with redundancy-reduced latent alignment, encouraging compact representations of risk-relevant relations in multi-source driving inputs. It further models vehicle control as residual action updates and uses residual-action sequence contrastive learning to align multi-step residual-driven rollouts with future latent states. A deterministic analysis shows that the latent-tanh residual parameterization preserves interior action reachability while representing smooth long-horizon control as compact local updates. Together, these designs improve risk-aware state abstraction, continuous-control modeling, and long-horizon dynamics prediction. Extensive experiments across diverse simulated driving scenarios demonstrate that LIDAR-AD consistently outperforms world-model baselines, achieving the highest reward and the best success rate among learning-based methods. Evaluations on nuPlan-derived log-reconstructed scenarios further demonstrate the transferability of LIDAR-AD under real-world traffic layouts.

</details>


### [161] [Beyond Coordinate Gauge: An Audited Protocol for Detecting Donor-Specific Functional Fingerprints after Neural Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11967)
*Truong Xuan Khanh,Phan Thanh Duc*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了独立训练的神经网络在收敛至神经坍缩状态后，其功能差异是否仍可被检测。通过五组在MNIST上重建神经坍缩的独立网络，采用经过验证的仿射校正对齐方法将供体网络头映射到受体坐标系中，发现供体特异性功能指纹在受体基线校正后依然可区分：所有20个有序供体-受体配对均被正确识别，置换检验p=0.0083，且对泄漏审计具有鲁棒性。结果支持可检测性，但未验证可移植性或因果持久性。研究展示了对齐、模糊性诊断与泄漏控制如何协同在受控环境下测试跨网络的功能差异，其外推性尚待验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 独立训练的神经网络缺乏共享的神经元索引参考框架，导致比较困难；而神经坍缩现象使网络趋于共享的低维几何结构，引发疑问：轨迹特定的功能差异在收敛后是否仍可区分。

Method: 使用五组独立训练的网络在MNIST数据集上重建神经坍缩，应用经过验证的仿射校正对齐方法将供体网络头部映射至受体坐标系，并进行基线校正与置换检验以评估功能指纹的可区分性。

Result: 所有20个供体-受体配对均被正确识别，置换检验p=0.0083，结果对泄漏审计具有鲁棒性，表明供体特异性功能指纹在对齐后仍可检测。

Conclusion: 研究证实了在所用测试条件下功能差异的可检测性，但未证明可移植性或因果持久性；对齐、模糊性诊断和泄漏控制的结合为跨网络功能变异的可控测试提供了方法，其泛化能力有待进一步研究。

Abstract: Independently trained neural networks have no shared neuron-index reference frame, so comparing them requires accounting for coordinate freedom. Neural Collapse sharpens this problem: networks converge toward a shared, low-dimensional geometry, raising the question of whether trajectory-specific functional variation remains distinguishable after convergence. We distinguish three claims - detectability, transplantability, and causal persistence - and address the first. Using five independently trained networks reconstructing Neural Collapse on MNIST, we apply a verified affine-correct alignment mapping donor heads into recipient coordinates. Donor-specific functional fingerprints remain distinguishable after recipient-level baseline correction: all 20 ordered donor-recipient pairs are correctly identified, with an exact permutation p=0.0083, robust to a leakage audit. These findings establish detectability under the test used here, but not transplantability or causal persistence. The study shows how alignment, ambiguity diagnostics, and leakage control combine to test cross-network variation in a controlled setting; whether this generalizes beyond it is open.

### [162] [Self-Evolving In-Context Learning for Direct Pilot-to-Beamformer Design in MU-MISO Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11970)
*Yubo Zhang,Xiaodong Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种增强的上下文学习（ICL）框架，用于提升多用户多输入单输出（MU-MISO）系统中基于导频的波束成形性能。该框架结合了ICL-Transformer主干网络、导频编码器-解码器网络（EDN）和波束成形器EDN，能够无需重新训练即可处理多种信道模型，通过构建特定于模型的上下文数据集实现。为提升收敛性和鲁棒性，引入三项关键创新：(a) 从监督式LMMSE模仿到无监督和速率最大化的课程学习策略；(b) 自我进化机制，动态扩展和优化所有信道模型的上下文数据集；(c) 匹配感知扩展，将多种失配情况融入通用ICL框架，避免显式信道校准。消融实验验证了上下文架构和增强训练策略的有效性。仿真结果表明，该方案能在不进行梯度更新的情况下快速适应已见与未见信道模型，并通过智能上下文构造缓解失配问题，且在基于导频的设置下持续优于现有波束成形方法，包括WMMSE基准和近期基于Transformer的方法。

Method: 采用ICL-Transformer作为主干网络，结合导频编码器-解码器网络（EDN）与波束成形器EDN，构建上下文学习框架。通过设计模型特定的上下文数据集实现对多信道模型的零样本适应。训练阶段引入课程学习策略，逐步从监督学习过渡到无监督优化；同时引入自进化机制，动态生成并优化上下文数据集；最后通过匹配感知扩展，将多种信道失配情形纳入统一框架，实现无需显式校准的鲁棒波束成形。

Result: 所提方案在多种通信环境下均表现出优异性能，可在不进行梯度更新的前提下快速适应已见与未见信道模型，有效缓解信道失配问题。相比传统WMMSE方法及当前先进的Transformer基波束成形方法，在和速率等指标上均有显著提升，展现出更强的泛化能力和实时适应性。

Abstract: We develop an enhanced in-context learning (ICL) framework to improve the performance of pilot-based beamforming in multi-user multiple-input single-output (MU-MISO) systems. The proposed scheme integrates the ICL-Transformer backbone with the pilot encoder-decoder network (EDN) and the beamformer EDN. A crucial feature of our ICL network is that it can handle multiple channel models without retraining, enabled by the construction of model-specific context datasets. To improve convergence and robustness, we introduce three key innovations: (a) a curriculum learning (CL) strategy that smoothly transitions from supervised LMMSE-labeled imitation to unsupervised sum-rate maximization, (b) a self-evolving mechanism that dynamically expands and refines the context datasets for all channel models during CL-based training, and (c) a mismatch-aware extension that incorporates several mismatches into the general ICL framework and bypasses explicit channel calibrations. Ablation studies validate the effectiveness of the in-context architecture and enhanced training strategies. Simulation results over diverse communication environments show that the proposed scheme is able to rapidly adapt to both seen and unseen channel models without gradient-based parameter updates, and can mitigate the mismatch issues via intelligent context constructions. Furthermore, our scheme consistently outperforms the existing beamforming schemes under pilot-based settings, including the WMMSE benchmark and the recent Transformer-based methods.

### [163] [Learning to Discretize: Diffusion-Based Adaptive Mesh with Spectral Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11974)
*Zixuan Shen,Bingchuan Wang,Zhi Wang,Yong Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于扩散模型的两阶段框架，用于学习神经偏微分方程（PDE）求解中的自适应网格离散化。第一阶段通过物理约束的条件生成学习网格位移，第二阶段基于优化后的网格表示预测场演化。通过引入物理感知代理通道、几何有效性约束和局部谱集中正则化，确保生成网格在物理上可解释且数值合法。在五个典型PDE场景中，该方法表现优于固定网格与手工设计网格方案，尤其在传统方法失效的复杂结构区域优势显著。结论强调：不存在通用最优网格规则，离散化应根据具体物理场景学习，将自适应网格构建从启发式问题转变为生成式表征学习任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经PDE代理模型依赖预设网格，而网格选择隐含地决定了建模能力在空间、分辨率和频带上的分配，这种设计选择无法动态调整，限制了模型对复杂物理结构的适应能力。因此，提出让网格本身可学习，以实现更灵活、高效的建模。

Method: 提出一个两阶段扩散模型框架：第一阶段以观测动力学为条件，生成r-自适应的网格位移；第二阶段利用该网格信息进行场演化预测。网格生成过程受到物理感知代理通道、几何合法性约束和局部谱集中度的联合正则化，确保生成结果既符合物理规律又满足数值稳定性要求。

Result: 在五个不同类型的PDE系统上验证，所提方法在预测精度和计算效率上均达到或超过自适应网格和降维基线方法的表现，尤其在传统固定或人工设计网格难以应对的复杂结构区域展现出显著优势。

Conclusion: 自适应网格不应被视为固定的求解器启发式，而应作为可学习的生成式表征过程。不同物理场景下的空间与频域结构差异意味着最优离散化策略具有强场景依赖性，因此需采用基于数据驱动的学习方式来动态生成网格。

Abstract: Most neural partial differential equation (PDE) surrogates learn how fields evolve after a grid has already been chosen. However, before any operator is applied, the grid has already determined how modeling capacity is allocated across space, resolution, and spectral bandwidth. We argue that this hidden design choice should itself be learnable, leading to a question different from standard operator learning: can a surrogate learn where resolution should exist before predicting field evolution? We formulate adaptive discretization as a physics-constrained conditional generation problem over valid mesh displacements. The success of diffusion models in PDE field prediction suggests their potential for learning adaptive discretizations under similar structured constraints. This leads to a two-stage diffusion framework: Stage 1 learns an r-adaptive displacement mesh conditioned on the observed dynamics, while Stage 2 predicts the solution evolution from the mesh-informed representation. The mesh generator is regularized by physics-aware proxy channels, geometric validity constraints, and local spectral concentration so that adaptation remains physically interpretable and numerically legal. Across five PDE regimes, the results show that diffusion-based learned discretization is competitive with adaptive-mesh and reduced-order baselines, with particularly strong gains in regimes where fixed or handcrafted allocation is insufficient. The main conclusion is not that there exists a universal optimal mesh rule, but that discretization should be learned in a regime-dependent manner: different spatial and spectral structures favor different allocation behaviors. This reframes adaptive meshing for neural PDE solvers from a solver-specific heuristic into a generative representation-learning problem.

In this paper, we propose GSUO, a guidance-signal-aware unlearning optimization framework that designs task-specific fine-grained guidance signals to steer the unlearning process and is applicable to both random-subset and class-wise forgetting tasks. ### [165] [LiteTopK: Exploiting the Curse of Dimensionality for a Fused Indexer-TopK Kernel in Long-Context Sparse Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11976)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过采样小规模数据估计查询-数据得分范围，利用该估计在线划分候选结果为多个桶，构建紧致的近似阈值，仅保留并写回有希望的候选者，从而减少无效内存操作和整体内存占用。

Abstract: Indexer-TopK, the operation to compute the scores and select the top-k candidates, is widely used by sparse attention kernels in large language models and vector retrieval in recommendation systems and vector databases. However, existing GPU-based Indexer-TopK kernels like DeepSeek Sparse Attention (DSA) remain inefficient due to excessive global memory traffic, costly synchronization, and prohibitive memory overhead. In this work, we exploit the curse of dimensionality in high-dimensional spaces, where distances between high-dimensional vectors tend to concentrate within a narrow range, to design LITETOPK, a novel and efficient fused Indexer-TopK kernel. LITETOPK first samples a small subset of data to estimate query-data score ranges, then uses these estimates to partition candidate results into bins online. This organization allows the LITETOPK kernel to maintain a tight approximate threshold, write back only promising candidates, reduce unnecessary I/O, substantially lower memory overhead, and still preserve exact Top-k correctness. Experimental results show that LITETOPK accelerates the prefill stage of GLM 5.2 by 1.2x in real-world deployment scenarios while incurring lower memory overhead.

### [167] [Sparse Inter-Layer Dependencies of Transformer FFN Neurons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11990)
*Johannes Knittel,Hanspeter Pfister*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种无需训练的归因方法，用于分析Transformer中前馈网络（FFN）神经元激活的上游影响因素。研究表明，少量前置神经元激活和注意力输出即可高保真地维持目标神经元的激活状态，即使其他输入被平均值掩码。在考虑上游层固有的激活稀疏性后，有效稀疏性进一步增强。同时在多层应用神经元特异性掩码时，模型困惑度在中等稀疏度下基本不变，表明FFN在神经元层面具有稀疏且结构化的层间依赖关系。该方法为电路级可解释性提供了实用、可扩展的工具，并识别出可能对高效推理有重要意义的稀疏路径。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer架构中的前馈网络（FFN）占用了大量参数和计算资源，但其内部结构因残差流的加性叠加而难以解释。理解FFN神经元激活的驱动因素对于提升模型可解释性和优化效率至关重要。

Method: 提出一种训练-free的归因方法，通过估计上游神经元和注意力输出对目标神经元激活的相对影响，评估哪些输入对激活贡献最大。通过掩码其余输入并保持平均值，量化关键输入的贡献。结合多层协同掩码，考察其对整体模型性能的影响。

Result: 实验结果表明，仅需少量前置激活和注意力输出即可高保真重建目标神经元激活；在考虑上游层固有的激活稀疏性后，稀疏性更显著；在多层同时应用神经元特异性掩码时，模型困惑度在中等稀疏度下几乎不变。

Conclusion: 尽管参数密集，FFN在神经元层面表现出稀疏且结构化的层间依赖关系。所提出的归因方法为电路级可解释性提供了一种高效、可扩展的工具，有助于发现潜在的稀疏推理路径。

Abstract: Feedforward network (FFN) blocks account for a large fraction of the parameters and computation in Transformer architectures, yet their internal structure remains difficult to interpret due to the additive superposition induced by the residual stream. We examine whether the activation of an FFN neuron can be explained by a sparse set of preceding neuron activations and attention outputs. We introduce a training-free attribution method that estimates the relative influence of upstream neurons and attention outputs on a target neuron's activation. Empirically, across models and layers, we find that small subsets of preceding activations and attention outputs suffice to preserve neuron activations with high fidelity when all remaining inputs are masked with their average values. Effective sparsity is even greater when accounting for the inherent activation sparsity of upstream layers. Moreover, applying the neuron-specific masks in all layers simultaneously, such that the induced deviations propagate through the network, leaves model perplexity largely unchanged at moderate sparsity levels. These results demonstrate that, despite dense parameterization, FFNs exhibit sparse and structured inter-layer dependencies at the neuron level. Our method provides a practical, scalable tool for circuit-level interpretability and identifies candidate sparse pathways with potential implications for efficient inference.

This paper proposes a Hierarchy-Aware RoBERTa framework that explicitly incorporates CWE structural information through learnable parent-class embeddings, preserving taxonomic consistency. ### [169] [Are we Merging the Right Models? Impact of Expert Training Duration on Model Merging for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11997)
*Nikita Kozodoi,Zainab Afolabi,Jack Butler*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究挑战了多任务模型合并中在最优验证损失时合并专家模型的常规做法，系统分析了训练时长对合并模型质量的影响。通过在五个领域（数学、代码、指令遵循、多语言和安全）上对三种规模的Qwen模型进行微调，并在25%到500%的最优训练步数范围内保存检查点，评估五种合并方法的表现。结果发现：简单平均法随过拟合恶化明显，而基于稀疏化的合并方法在超过验证最优时表现最佳。通过偏差-方差分解分析，揭示其与随机森林中高方差个体学习器的优势类似，表明训练时长与合并方法应联合选择而非独立决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标准做法是在专家模型达到最优验证损失时进行合并，但该研究质疑这一惯例，旨在探索训练持续时间对合并后模型性能的影响，以优化多任务模型合并策略。

Result: 简单平均合并方法在过拟合时性能显著下降，而稀疏化合并方法在超过验证最优训练步数时表现最佳；偏差-方差分析显示，这与随机森林中高方差模型的优势机制相似，说明合并策略需与训练时长协同设计。

Conclusion: 训练时长与合并方法的选择应联合考虑，不能孤立决策。特别是对于稀疏化合并方法，延长训练时间可提升合并模型性能，从而打破传统在验证最优时合并的局限性。

Abstract: Multi-task model merging combines separately trained expert models into a single model that handles all tasks without co-training. Standard practice merges experts at their optimal validation loss. We challenge this convention by systematically studying how training duration of domain experts affects the quality of the merged model. We fine-tune experts on five domains (Math, Code, Instruction Following, Multilingual, and Safety) across three model sizes (Qwen 3.5 0.8B, 2B, and 4B), saving checkpoints from 25\% to 500\% of the optimal training steps and evaluating five merging methods at each duration. Our findings reveal a striking method-dependent pattern: simple averaging degrades sharply with overfitting, while sparsification-based methods achieve their best performance well past the validation optimum. We formalize this through bias-variance decomposition analysis, drawing a parallel to random forests where averaging benefits from high-variance individual learners. These results suggest that training duration and merging method should be chosen jointly rather than independently.

### [172] [PFAdapter: Hierarchical LoRA Decomposition for Personalized Federated MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12111)
*Jing Liu,Kun Yang,Yan Wang,Dingkang Yang,Xiaoshuai Hao,Wei Zhang,Yang Liu,Wei Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PFAdapter 是一种通信高效的联邦微调框架，通过层次化 LoRA 分解将适配器参数分为全局共享和本地私有部分，分别处理跨网络的通用多模态语义与边缘特定适应。通过仅同步全局组件并引入基于 Frobenius 范数的正交性约束，显著降低通信开销（近 50%），同时提升个性化性能。在 VQA-RAD、SLAKE、Hateful Memes 和 CrisisMMD 等数据集上，相比现有方法准确率提升 2.4%–4.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦微调方法在异构网络条件下难以平衡全局知识聚合与本地个性化，且统一参数聚合导致特征冗余与高通信成本，限制了多模态大模型在边缘智能中的应用效率。

Method: 提出 PFAdapter 框架，采用层次化 LoRA 分解机制，将查询与键投影设为全局共享以捕捉通用多模态语义，值与输出投影保留在本地以实现边缘定制化；引入 Frobenius 范数正则化确保两部分严格分离；采用选择性聚合策略仅传输全局参数，减少通信开销。

Result: 在多个多模态任务数据集上，PFAdapter 显著优于当前主流基线方法，准确率提升 2.4% 至 4.8%，通信开销降低近 50%，有效支持资源受限网络中自主智能体的高效部署。

Conclusion: PFAdapter 为边缘智能场景下的多模态大模型联邦学习提供了一种高效、可扩展且隐私友好的解决方案，实现了高质量个性化与低通信成本的协同优化。

Within distributed network environments, Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) serve as cognitive engines for edge devices, yet federated fine-tuning faces substantial challenges in balancing global knowledge aggregation with local adaptation under heterogeneous network conditions. Conventional federated protocols typically rely on uniform parameter aggregation, which conflates domain-invariant features with client-specific nuances, thereby resulting in suboptimal personalization and excessive communication overhead. To address these challenges, we propose PFAdapter, a communication-efficient framework introducing hierarchical LoRA decomposition to explicitly separate adapter parameters into global-shared and local-private components. Query and key projections are assigned to global synchronization for capturing universal multimodal semantics across the network, while value and output projections remain localized for edge-specific adaptation. Additionally, orthogonality regularization based on the Frobenius norm enforces strict separation between these components, preventing redundant feature learning. Selective aggregation protocols synchronize only global-shared components across the federated network, preserving local expertise and reducing communication costs by nearly 50%. Extensive experiments on VQA-RAD, SLAKE, Hateful Memes, and CrisisMMD datasets demonstrate that PFAdapter consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving accuracy improvements ranging from 2.4% to 4.8% across diverse edge intelligence tasks. Consequently, our framework establishes an efficient solution for agentic AI deployment in resource-constrained communication networks.

Abstract: Federated fine-tuning of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) across distributed networks enables privacy-sensitive adaptation to evolving data streams, yet a fundamental obstacle prevents robust deployment in dynamic environments: catastrophic forgetting, wherein sequential task updates erase previously acquired knowledge across visual, linguistic, and cross-modal representations. Addressing this challenge is especially critical for autonomous networked AI operating in safety-sensitive domains, such as content moderation, where reliable retention of prior knowledge underpins system integrity. To overcome this, we propose Federated Continual Multimodal Learning (FedCMM), a framework that embeds continual-learning safeguards into the federated optimization loop at three complementary levels. At the parameter level, modality-aware elastic weight consolidation computes separate Fisher information matrices for the vision encoder, language backbone, and cross-modal projector, providing granular, asymmetry-aware protection against modality-specific forgetting. At the data level, each client trains a lightweight local generative replay module to synthesize raw-data-free embedding-level multimodal replay tuples without any raw data sharing. At the aggregation level, Task-similarity-aware gradient aggregation autonomously filters and reweights client updates by gradient cosine similarity, suppressing conflicting directions and stabilizing the global learning trajectory. Extensive experiments on two benchmarks demonstrate that FedCMM consistently outperforms recent baselines on accuracy and backward transfer, confirming that holistic, modality-aware optimization enables robust evolutive adaptation across heterogeneous networked AI deployments.

### [174] [An Agentic AI Scientific Community for Automated Neural Operator Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12122)

Method: 构建一个由虚拟实验室组成的群体智能系统，每个实验室包含三个代理：LLM规划者（生成架构）、数值工作者（训练与评估）、LLM评审者（跨实验室同行评审）。采用引用经济机制驱动实验室演化，支持多种基础算子模块的混合设计，并通过多轮仿真与审计验证性能与可解释性。

Result: 在5个典型问题（包括1D/2D PDE）上均成功发现高精度、低参数量的神经算子架构；99.8%的架构决策为多家族混合结构；规则基替代实验导致系统退化为单一家族堆叠，证明LLM代理对维持多样性至关重要。

Conclusion: 神经算子不存在万能最优解，需依赖多样化探索；基于LLM代理的自主科学共同体是实现高效、创新架构发现的有效范式。代码与完整日志已开源。

Abstract: We present an agentic approach to autonomous neural operator discovery based on an AI scientific community, which consists of a swarm of virtual laboratories that interact under a citation-based economy of influence. Highly-cited labs found new labs that follow their research direction and replace non-performing labs. Each virtual lab contains three agents: an LLM planner that proposes an architecture, a numerical worker that trains and measures it, and an LLM reviewer that participates in cross-lab peer review. All labs share a common vocabulary consisting of DeepONet (branch-trunk), Fourier, Transformer (attention), wavelet, and residual convolutional neural operator building blocks. We evaluate the neural operator AI scientific community on five problems, namely piecewise regression, the linear advection and Burgers 1D PDEs, and the Navier-Stokes and Darcy flow 2D PDEs, while repeating the simulation three times for each problem. The results show that the neural operator AI scientific community is capable of discovering high-accuracy, low-parameter-count neural operator architectures. All 9,623 LLM calls are logged and audited, which reveals that the virtual lab LLM planners choose to hybridize in 99.8% of their logged decisions, consistently returning multi-family hybrids. Moreover, we conducted an ablation study by replacing the LLM agents in each lab by rule-based alternatives, which caused the scientific community to collapse to non-hybridized single-family stacks in several cases, showing that LLM agency is needed to preserve diversity. The results suggest a no-free-lunch theorem for neural operators: there is no universal winner. The code, configurations, and the complete LLM transcripts are released at https://github.com/luislootx/AI-SC.

</details>


### [175] [From Geometric Recovery to Causal Validation: A Reproducible Audit of Sparse Autoencoder Features, from Superposition Geometry to Causal Inertness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12166)
*Mohamed Abdessalem Bal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了稀疏自编码器（SAE）评估中依赖相关性恢复指标的局限性，指出其混淆了解码器几何对齐与编码器激活行为两个不同命题。通过复现经典实验并引入因果审计方法（sae-causal-audit），发现高达77%的高相关性特征在实际中并无因果作用，即特征存在但对应原子不激活。进一步分析表明，这种惰性可分解为结构性惰性和竞争性惰性，并区分读取与写入惰性，且部分特征虽无法通过消融检测却可通过引导操纵。研究还发现字节级复现不可行，建议以声明堆栈形式报告结果。应用于生产级SAE时，在小规模下仍观察到14%的惰性特征，并发现原子碰撞信号：少数原子反复匹配多个无关概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SAE评估主要依赖解码器原子与真实方向间的余弦相似度，但该指标无法区分解码器几何对齐与编码器实际激活行为，导致对特征可解释性的误判。研究旨在揭示这一评估偏差，提出更严格的因果验证框架。

Method: 通过复现超叠加相图与TopK vs L1对比实验，引入因果审计工具sae-causal-audit，对每个恢复特征进行消融和引导测试；结合几何分析、多批次验证与原子匹配追踪，系统识别特征惰性来源及其类型。

Result: 发现高达77%的高相关性特征在降级SAE中为因果惰性，即使余弦接近1.000也未实际激活；良好SAE中仍有9%惰性；惰性可分解为结构性与竞争性，以及读取/写入惰性；发现原子碰撞现象，即少数原子匹配大量无关概念。

Conclusion: 当前基于相关性的SAE评估方法存在根本缺陷，需转向因果审计。提出的sae-causal-audit工具可有效识别特征惰性，揭示隐藏的几何与竞争性机制。应放弃字节级复现，改用带明确范围的声明堆栈报告结果。

Abstract: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) are the standard for decomposing superposed neural representations into interpretable features, and evaluation relies predominantly on correlational recovery metrics -- cosine similarity between ground-truth directions and decoder atoms. We show this conflates two distinct claims: decoder-geometry alignment and encoder-activation behavior. We reproduce the superposition phase diagram of Elhage et al. (2022), identifying a convergence artifact at high sparsity and an under-described diffuse sharing regime at extreme overcompleteness. We reproduce the TopK-versus-L1 comparison of Gao et al. (2024), with direct evidence of L1 shrinkage. Our central result is causal: subjecting every recovered feature to ablation and steering, we find up to 77% of features passing a recovery bar (cosine >= 0.90) in a degraded SAE -- and 9% in a well-trained one -- are causally inert: the matched atom never fires when the feature is present, including matches at cosine ~1.000. We package the method as sae-causal-audit, a model-agnostic instrument with a deterministic pipeline. Re-auditing refines the finding: inertness decomposes by cause into structural inertness (antipodal-pair geometry, present in good SAEs) and competitive inertness (a TopK pathology of degraded SAEs), and by direction into read- and write-inertness, which five antipodal pairs dissociate completely -- unmonitorable yet steerable through the same atom, with steering specificities of 143-310 attached to zero ablation effects. We document why byte-exact reproducibility is unavailable by construction, and propose reporting it as a stack of claims with explicit scopes. Applying the instrument to a production SAE reproduces the pattern at small scale (14% inert) and surfaces an atom-collision signal: a handful of atoms recur as the nearest match for dozens of unrelated concepts, replicated across three batches.

</details>


### [176] [Forgetful Attention: A Trainable Support-Vector Memory with Certified Selection and Exact Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12204)
*Vishwajith Ramesh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出支持向量注意力（SV-Attention），通过一分类SVM的权重系数实现可证明的令牌删除与精确编辑，支持在线学习中的记忆管理；实验显示其在保持输出不变性方面优于现有方法，在真实数据集上显著提升稀有项召回率并减少退化，同时在enwik8等任务中表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测试时记忆无法保证删除某个令牌后输出不变或完全消除其影响，需要一种能提供可证明删除能力的记忆机制。

Method: 引入支持向量注意力（SV-Attention），利用固定参数C的一类SVM的权重作为注意力权重，通过活动集划分使冗余令牌权重为零，实现输出保持的移除；采用可逆增量求解器恢复重训练状态，并使用定制反向传播实现精确路径计算。

Result: fp64实验中，减量与重拟合结果一致，决策函数偏差中位数约10^-9（键向量为10^-13），最差情况仅出现在病态重复项且始终低于系数衰减；训练效率达9,125 tokens/s，虽慢于参考实现但具备精确删除证书；在真实MIMIC-IV流中，认证选择的稀有项召回率达0.86（对比0.32），退化小时数降至0.80（对比0.05）；在enwik8上取得2.178 BPC，优于滑动窗口Transformer的2.383 BPC（8.6%改进，p=0.001）。

Conclusion: SV-Attention实现了可证明的令牌删除、精确编辑与手术式遗忘，在多个基准上展现出优越性能，为可解释、可控的注意力记忆提供了新范式。

Abstract: Attention can be viewed as an online learner over context, yet existing test-time memories cannot certify that dropping a token leaves outputs unchanged or delete its influence outright. We introduce Support Vector Attention (SV-Attention), a max-margin memory whose weights are support coefficients of a one-class SVM with fixed box parameter C. Its active-set partition gives reserve tokens exactly zero weight, certifying output-preserving eviction; a reversible incremental solver deletes a token to recover the state produced by retraining without it under the same C. In fp64 experiments, decrement and refit recover identical partitions whenever the optimum is unique, and their decision functions match to a median deviation of about 10^-9 (10^-13 on learned keys); the 10^-2 worst case is confined to ill-conditioned duplicates and remains below coefficient decay in every regime. The exact path reuses the maintained KKT inverse in a custom backward. Training uses a separate stabilized batched approximation and does not carry the exact-deletion certificate; it reaches 9,125 tokens/s on a 3.22M-parameter model, while remaining 35.8 times slower than an MPS softmax reference. At matched budgets, certified selection reaches 0.86 vs. 0.32 rare-item recall and retains 0.80 vs. 0.05 deterioration hours on real MIMIC-IV streams. We also demonstrate surgical forgetting, exact editing, patient-record deletion, and a forgettable retrieval memory over real sentence embeddings. On enwik8, the hybrid obtains 2.178 BPC vs. 2.383 for a matched-state sliding-window Transformer across seven seeds (8.6% paired improvement, p=0.001); a three-seed TinyStories result is directionally positive but not significant (p=0.057).
